<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wit.html>wit</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:loof.html>loof</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:witlof.html>witlof</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netherlands" class="extiw" title="w:Netherlands">Netherlands</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Belgian endive, <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Cichorium_intybus_subsp._foliosum" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Cichorium intybus subsp. foliosum"><i>Cichorium intybus</i> subsp. <i>foliosum</i></a></span>, a chicory eaten as a leafy vegetable</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:witt.html>witt</a> (50228)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">hwīt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hwītaz</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">hvid</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wit.html>wit</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">weiß</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">hvit</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">wyt</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">in several dialects, including  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_Prussian_dialect" class="extiw" title="w:Low Prussian dialect">Low Prussian</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> white</li>

***woede.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:woede.html>woede</a> (2365)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">woet</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*wuot</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*wuodi</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wōþuz</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Wut</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">anger, rage</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare the related adjective <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">wōd</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:raging.html>raging</a>, insane</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">wode</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">insane</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***woeden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:woeden.html>woeden</a> (42739)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:woeden.html>woeden</a></i>, a derivate of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">woet</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:woeden.html>woeden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to rage
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>Onder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:grote.html>Grote</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:brand.html>brand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:londen.html>Londen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verstaat.html>verstaat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vuurzee.html>vuurzee</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vanaf.html>vanaf</a> 2 september 1666 (Juliaanse <a href = vnd.unilang:kalender.html>kalender</a>), 12 september 1666 (<a href = vnd.unilang:gregoriaans.html>Gregoriaanse</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kalender.html>kalender</a>), <a href = vnd.unilang:gedurende.html>gedurende</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:drie.html>drie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dagen.html>dagen</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Engelse <a href = vnd.unilang:hoofdstad.html>hoofdstad</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:woedde.html>woedde</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:belangrijk.html>belangrijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deel.html>deel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>deze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:plaats.html>plaats</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verwoestte.html>verwoestte</a>.</i><sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>  |  By the Great Fire of London one understands the sea of fire which starting on 2 September 1666 (Julian calendar), 12 September 1666 (Gregorian calendar), raged for three days in the English capital and which destroyed an important part of this place.</dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:woekeren.html>woekeren</a></i>, derived from the noun <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:woekeren.html>woeker</a></i>. ***woensdag.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:woensdag.html>woensdag</a> (2932)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">woensdach</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*wuodenesdag</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*Wōdanas dagaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">day of Woden</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, calque of Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:dies.html>dies</a> Mercurii</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:woensdag.html>woensdag</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:woensdagen.html>woensdagen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:woensdag.html>woensdagje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>Wednesday</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:woest.html>woest</a> (5119)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:woeste.html>woeste</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wuosti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wōstijaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:woest.html>woest</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:woest.html>woester</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:woest.html>woest</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">woestst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>(<i>concerning a creature and behavior</i>) wild, savage, feral, ferocious, furious

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:woest.html>woest</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-e-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ling.html>ling</a></i>.

***woestijn.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:woestijn.html>woestijn</a> (2173)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">woestine</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wuostinna</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Wüste</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">waste</i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wolf.html>wolf</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:wulf.html>wulf</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*<a href = vnd.unilang:wulf.html>wulf</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wulfaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wĺ̥kʷos</i>.

***wolverine.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wolverine.html>wolverine</a> (17085)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>1619; alteration of earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">wolvering</i> (1574), diminutive of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">wolver</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ravenous or savage animal; person who behaves like a <a href = vnd.unilang:wolf.html>wolf</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (1593),<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> ultimately from <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wolf.html>wolf</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wolverine.html>wolverine</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wolverines.html>wolverines</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A solitary, fierce mammal of the Mustelidae family, <i><span class="Latn" lang="mul">Gulo gulo</span></i><sup><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Gulo_gulo" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Gulo gulo">ws</a></sup>.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1920</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Peter_B._Kyne" class="extiw" title="w:Peter B. Kyne"><a href = vnd.unilang:peter.html>Peter</a> B. Kyne</a>,  chapter IV, in  <cite>The Understanding Heart</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">“Wish I'd <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> more polite to that girl,” the <a href = vnd.unilang:sheriff.html>sheriff</a> remarked regretfully. “ I ain'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> a bite to eat since four <a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a>'clock this morning, and I'm hungry as a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wolverine.html>wolverine</a></b>. … I know she'd have give <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> another <a href = vnd.unilang:drink.html>drink</a> of that old <a href = vnd.unilang:moonshine.html>moonshine</a> she <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a>.”</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>carcajou, <a href = vnd.unilang:skunk.html>skunk</a> bear, glutton, quickhatch, beaver eater</li></ul>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wonde.html>wonde</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wunde</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wunda</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wundō</i>. <p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wonderlijc</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wunderlīk</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">wonder</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-lijk</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wonderlijk.html>wonderlijk</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wonderlijker.html>wonderlijker</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">wonderlijkst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>miraculous, amazing</li>
<li>queer, odd</li>
<li>vagarious</li></ol>

***woodcock.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:woodcock.html>woodcock</a> (55387)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">wodecocke</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">wode-koc</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">wodekok</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">wudecocc</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">wuducoc</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">wood</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cock</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:woodcock.html>woodcock</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:woodcock.html>woodcock</a></strong></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">woodcocks</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Any of several wading <a href = vnd.unilang:birds.html>birds</a> in the genus <i>Scolopax</i>, of the family Scolopacidae, characterised by a long slender bill and cryptic brown and blackish plumage.</li>
<li>A simpleton.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><abbr title="circa">c.</abbr></i> <b>1607–1611</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Francis_Beaumont" class="extiw" title="w:Francis Beaumont">Francis Beaumont</a> |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Fletcher_(playwright)" class="extiw" title="w:John Fletcher (playwright)">John <a href = vnd.unilang:fletcher.html>Fletcher</a></a>,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cupid%27s_Revenge" class="extiw" title="w:Cupid | s Revenge"><a href = vnd.unilang:cupid.html>Cupid</a>’s Revenge</a>”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Beaumont_and_Fletcher_folios" class="extiw" title="w:Beaumont and Fletcher folios">Comedies and <a href = vnd.unilang:tragedies.html>Tragedies</a><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="Written by Francis Beavmont and Iohn Fletcher Gentlemen. Never Printed before, and Now Published by the Authours Originall Copies.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></a></cite>, London |  Printed for <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Humphrey_Robinson" class="extiw" title="w:Humphrey Robinson">Humphrey Robinson</a>,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="at the Three Pidgeons">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, and for <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Humphrey_Moseley" class="extiw" title="w:Humphrey Moseley">Humphrey Moseley</a><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="at the Princes Armes in St Pauls Church-yard.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, published 1679, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/3083972">3083972</a></small>, Act 4, scene 1:</span><dl><dd></dd></dl></div>
<dl><dd>If I <a href = vnd.unilang:loved.html>loved</a> you not, I would laugh at you, and see you / Run your neck into the <a href = vnd.unilang:noose.html>noose</a>, and cry, "A <b><a href = vnd.unilang:woodcock.html>woodcock</a></b>!"</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1838</b>, Nathan <a href = vnd.unilang:drake.html>Drake</a>, <i>Belletristical Works</i> (volume 1, page 215)
<dl><dd>"Now will that silly <b><a href = vnd.unilang:woodcock.html>woodcock</a></b> make such a report of what I have <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> to his chosen friend," observed <a href = vnd.unilang:sir.html>Sir</a> Robert to his companion when my Lord Cobham <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> out of hearing<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>

</p>

</p>
<ol><li>any group of <a href = vnd.unilang:houses.html>houses</a> with a distinct name and identity, regardless of size; includes <a href = vnd.unilang:hamlets.html>hamlets</a>, villages, <a href = vnd.unilang:towns.html>towns</a>, cities and so on</li>
<li>habitat, place of residence</li></ol>
